4a1(1): ye shes kyi ming badza// zhi ba'i snying po nga/ ting nge 'dzin gyi snying po dang / bad+ma'i snying po dang / rnam par grol ba'i thab dang / kun du rdza ba dang / drug
4a2(1): dang / mthutshan thob dang / kun du bzang po dang / kun nas mig dang / bad+ma'i tshig dang / drim med pa'i tshig dang / yangs pa'i mig dang / gung du myed lam dang / kun tu mdzes
4a3(1): blo gros dang / ye shes kyi blo gros dang / chos kyi blo gros dang / rgyal ba'i blos dang / bla ma'i blo gros dang / rdo rje'i blo gros dang / khyang par blo gros dang / seng ge rnam par rol pa na pa
4a4(1): dbyangs kyi rgyal po dang / seng ge'i sgra sgrogs dang / sgra dbyangs brjod pa bzab mo sgrog dang / gos pa med pa dang / dri ma kun bral dang / zla ba'i 'od dang / nyi ma'i 'od dang / ye
4a5(1): ye shes dpal dang / bzang po'i dpal dang zla ba'i dpal dang / badz+ra'i dpal dang / drin mo cha'i dpal dang / 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa dang / bzums sngags
4a6(1): skyes bu dam pa bcu drug dang / byams pa la sogs pa bskal pa bzang po'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po thams cad dang / rgyal po chen po bani la sogs pa ma chen po ni ras kyi
4a7(1): slong brnams dpa/ ga'i dbang ba kyi byin la sags pa su cu cu gsum ris kyi lha'i burnams dang / lha'i bung ba 'tha' rnal la legs pa 'tha ba bral kyi lha'i bu rnams dang tu bu rangs
4b1(1): dga' ldan la sogs pa dga' ldan gyi ris kyi lha'i bu rnams dang / lha'i bu rab 'phrul dga' la sogs pa 'phrul dga'i ris kyi lha'i bu rnams dang / lha'i bu dbang byed la sogs pa gzhan
4b2(1): 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha'i bu rnams dang / ded dpon la sogs pa dkar po'i phyogs bdud kyi bu rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po la sogs pa tshangs ris kyi lha'i bu rnams dang / lha'i bu dbang phyug
4b3(1): chen po la sogs pa gnas gtsang ma'i ris kyi lha'i bu thams cad dang / lha ma yin gyi dbang po thag bzangs ris dang / stobs can dang / sgra can dang / de dag la sogs pa lnga ma yin brgya
4b4(1): stong phrag du ma dang / klu'i rgyal po ma dros pa dang / gzi can dang / rgya mtsho dang / mtha' yas dang / nor rgyas kyi bu dang / de dag la sogs pa klu'i rgyal po rgya stong du ma dang / dpal gyi
4b5(1): gzi brjid la sogs pa klu'i rgyal po'i khye'u brgya stong du ma dang / klu'i bu mo mang po rnams dang / de ma yin pa gzhan lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / lA ma yin dang / nam
4b6(1): mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po dang / mi dang mi ma yin pa dag gis ma gang bar gyur pa'i sa phyogs sam/ mar snang gi phyogs de med do// 'khor de lta bu 'dus shing
4b7(1): brgya stong dang yang thabs cig go/ yang de'i g.yan ga ya'i mgo'i ri'i dpag chad bzhi khor khor yug tu// skra'i rtse mo'i cha shas kyi rdul za rab tsam yang gang lha dang / ku dang / gnod sbyid
6a1(1): nam mkha'i khams thams cad kyi gseb phye ba 'am/ btsums par mi mngon pa de bzhin du/ de'i tshe na 'od gzer de dag zhugs kyang bcom ldan 'das kyis zhal gyi sgo phye ba
6a2(1): 'am/ btsums par yang mi mngon no// 'di lta ste dper nadabye ma'i phung po la mar ram/ 'bru mar ram/ chu nags na mi mngon pa de bzhin du de'i tshe na 'od zer de dag zhugs kyang bye ba 'am/ 
6a3(1): btsums par mi mngon no// de nas shar phyogs su sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'di nas/ 'jig rten gyi khams gang+gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed 'das pa dang / bad+ma can zhes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams de na de bani/ 
6a4(1): gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rig pa dang rkang par ldan pa/ bde bar gshegs pa/ 'jig rten mkhyen pa/ skyes bu 'dul ba'i kha lo sgyur ba/ bla na med pa/ 
6a5(1): dang mi rnams kyi smon pa/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das pad+ma'i spyan zhes bya ba de byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams la 'di lta ste/ theg pa gcig las btsams nas/ chos
6a6(1): rgan te sangs rgyas kyi ning de mnyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas dge dang / nyan thos kyi theg pa 'am/ rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa'i ming yang med/ sangs rgyas kyi ning chen brdzus te
6a7(1): ma chogs par bud med dang mngalan gnas te 'byung zhing skye ba'i sgra yang mi grag go// 'jig rten gyi khams na'i sems can de dag thams cad kyang / bla na med yang dag par rdzog pa'i byang chuba'
6b1(1): pir pi ldog pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sha stag go// 'jig rten gyi khams de na gzanga' ba dang / btung ba dang zas kyi bya ba yang mi shes so// byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyang
6b2(1): bsam gtan gyi dga' ba'i zas can dang / ting nge 'dzin gyi dga' ba'i zas can dang / chos kyi dga' ba'i zas can no// de bzhin gshegs pa de nyid kyi 'od kyis 'jig rten gyi khams de khyab
6b3(1): cing / dri ma med par gyur pa ma rtogs par 'jig rten gyi khams de na zla ba dang nyi ma dang / gza' dang skar pa rnams kyi 'od kyang mi shes so// 'jig rten gyi khams de lag mthil bzhin du mnyam
6b4(1): par gyur pa las/ 'jig rten gyi khams de na rtsa ba dang / shing dang / bong ba dang / rtsig pa dang / ri la sogs pa yang mi snang ngo / 'jig rten gyi khams de 'dra bden byang chub sems dpa'
6b5(1): sems dpa' chen po bsgrib pa thams cad rnam par sel ba zhes bya ba de'i ming thos pa tsam gyis/ sems can gyi bsgrib pa thams cad zad par 'gyur ba zhig gnas te/ de 'od des reg ste bskul nas
6b6(1): rang gi gnas nas byung ste/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa bad+ma'i spyan de ga la ba der song ste/ phyin nas bcom ldan 'das de'i zhabs pa mgo bos phyag 'tshal te/ pad+ma'i snying po la phyogs gcig
6b7(1): tu 'dug go// de ma yin pa'i byang chub sems dpa' gzhan dag kyang 'od reg ste bskul bar dang / rang rang gi gnas byung ste/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa pad+ma'i sman ga la ba der
7a1(1): dang sa phyin nas bcom ldan 'das de'i zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal te/ pad+ma'i snying po la ma ma tsha rigs par 'khod do// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po
7a2(1): slob pa thams cad rnam par sel ba bstan las langs te// bla gos zag pa gcig tu gzangs/ pus mo g.yas pa'i ldangs la gtsugs te/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa pad+ma'i snyun ga la
7a3(1): ba der logs su thal mo sbyar bdud nas/ bcom ldan 'das de la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das 'di lta bu'i 'od bzang po rngom ma mchis pa rnam par dag pa yid du mchis pa lus dang
7a4(1): sems shin tu dga' bar bgyid pa/ byang ba 'di su'i lags shes de skad ces gsol pa dang / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa pad+ma'i spyan des byang chub sems dpa' sgrib pa thams
7a5(1): cad rnam par sel ba la/ 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rigs kyi bu nub phyogs na sangs rgyas kyi ning 'di nas 'jig rten gyi khams gang+gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed 'das pa na mi mjed ces bya ba'i
7a6(1): 'jig rten gyi khams lad de/ de na de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rig pa dang rkang par ldan pa/ bde bar gshegs pa/ 'jig rten mkhyen pa/ 
7b1(1): skyes bu 'dul ba/ kha lo sbyar ba/ bla na med pa/ lha dang mi rnams kyi ston pa/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa zhes bya ba de de'i mtshan thos pa tsam gyis sems can rnams blar med ba lang
7b2(1): dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi ldog par 'gyur ba zhig bzhugs te/ des 'od bzang po dri ma med pa/ rnam par dag pa yid du 'ong ba/ lus dang sems shin tu dga' bar byed pa 'di byung ngo
7b3(1): de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa pad+ma'i spyan de la/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sgrib pa thams cad rnam par sel bas 'di skad ces gsol to// 
7b4(1): bcom ldan 'das de ltar de bzhin gshegs pa de'i mtshan thos pa tsam gyis sems can rnams bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi log par 'gyur ba'i rgyu gang lags/ rkyen gang
7b5(1): lags/ de skad ces gsol pa dang / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa pad+ma'i spyan des byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sgrib pa thams cad rnam par gsol ba la 'di skad ces bka
7b6(1): stsal to// rigs kyi bu de bzhin gshegs pa des sngon byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa spyod pa na 'di ltar sems can su gang dag gis bdag mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas pa'i ming thos pa de dag
7b7(1): thams cad bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi ldog par shog shig ces smon lam btab bo// byang chub sems dpa' sgrib pa thams cad rnam par sel bas gsol pa/ 
8a1(1): bcom ldan 'das ci lags/ 'jig rten gyi khams de'i sems can de dag thams cad phyir mi ldog pa lags sam/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ 
8a2(1): rigs kyi bu ma yin no// byang chub sems dpa' sgrib thams cad rnam par sel bas gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das ci lags sems can de dag gis de bzhin gshegs pa de'i char mi thos
8a3(1): sam/ bcom ldan 'das des bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu thos so// gsol ba bcom ldan 'das de ci'i slad du phyir mi ldog pa lags sam/ bcom ldan 'das des bka' stsal
8a4(1): rigs kyi bu de dag thams cad ni phyir mi ldog pa yang yin la/ phyir mi ldog pa'ang ma yin no// gsol ba bcom ldan 'das ji ltar gang lta bu de dag thams cad phyir mi ldog pa yang
8a5(1): legs la/ phyir mi ldog pa yang ma lags/ bcom ldan 'das des bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan thos pas sems can de dag gi phyir mi ldog pa'i
8a6(1): sa bon skyes pa mthong nas sems can de dag phyir mi ldog par lung spyod to// mtshan thos pa khe nas de ma thag tu de dag gi phyir mi ldog par 'gyur ba yang ma yin te/ de bas na rigs kyi
8a7(1): bungan pa nyid rab tu grub par bya ba'i phyir/ khyod la dpe bshad do// rigs kyi bu 'di la sted par da shing la langs ben gyi nyes pa thams cad med la/ s+ya gu skye ba nas rdzogs pa
8b1(1): bar du rkyen rnams yod na// rigs kyi bu sa bon de la ci skad ces bya/ gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das nyes pa thams cad dang bral bas na/ de ni yongs su rdzogs pa zhes bgyi'o// bka' stsal pa
8b2(1): rigs kyi bu de bzhin du de bzhin shegs pa'i mtshan thos pa dang ldan pa'i phyir mi ldog pa'i sa bon yod pa'i sems can rnams na bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir
8b3(1): mi ldog pa yin no// de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang // bcom lngas 'das de bzhin shegs pa pad ma'i spyan de la byang chub sems dpa' chen po sgrib pa thams cad rnam par sel ba
8b4(1): 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag mi mjed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams de lta ba dang // bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs
8b5(1): pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa de la'ang phyag 'tshal ba dang / bsnyen bkur ba dang / btsun par bgyi ba dang / ri mor bgyi ba dang / bkur sti bgyi ba dang / mchod par bgyi ba'i sdang
8b6(1): du mchi'o// de skad ces gsol pa dang / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa pad ma'i spyan des byang chub sems dpa' chen po sgrib pa thams cad rnam sel ba la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// 
8b7(1): rigs kyi bu de'i dus la bab par shes na khyod song shig/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa pad ma'i spyan de la byang chub sems dpa' di dag thams cad kyis kyang 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom
9a1(1): / ldan 'das bdag cag kyang mi mjed kyi 'jig rten gyi khas de lta ba dang / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa de la phyag 'tshal ba dang / 
9a2(1): bsnyen bkur gyi ba dang / btsun par bgyi ba dang / ri mor bgyi ba dang / bkur sti gyi ba dang / mchod par bgyi ba'i skang du mchi'o// de skad ces stsol ba dang / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pad+ma'i spyan des byang chub sem
9a3(1): dpa' de dag la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rigs kyi bu de'i dus la dab par shes na khyed deng shig/ 'jig rten gyi khams der ngag yod par gnas pas gnas par gyis shig/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar
9a4(1): 'jig rten gyi khams de'i sems gang dag ni rab tu 'dod chags mang ba/ zhe sdang mang ba/ gti mug mang ba/ dge sbyong du mi 'dzin pa/ bram zer mi 'dzin pa/ par mi 'dzin pa/ mar mi 'dzin pa/ chos ma yin pa 'dod pa
9a5(1): brlang ba/ gtum pa/ zhe gcod pa/ mu cor sgru ba po theg can/ g.yengs pa/ brkam pa/ le lo can/ tshul khrims 'chal pa/ sdig pa'i chos can/ pra drog dang ser snas yongs su dkris pa/ nyon mongs
9a6(1): bdams nye bar nyon mongs par gyur pa rnams te/ sems can de 'dra ba de dag gi nang na de bzhin gshegs de chos ston to// byang chub sems dpa' de dag gis gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das gang 'di 'dra ma
9a7(1): sems can rnams kyi nang na chos ston pa ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa de dka' ba mdzad pa lags so// bcom ldan 'das kyis bku stsal pa/ de de bzhin no// rigs kyi bu de de bzhin te/ gang 'di 'dra ba'i sems can rnams
9b1(1): kyi nang na chos ston pa ni de bzhin gshegs pa de bka' ba 'jangad pa yin no// rigs bla dag de lta bur kun nas nyon mongs par gyur pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams na dge ba'i sems gcig tsam bskyed pa'i sems can de dag kyang bka' bzed
9b2(1): pa yin no// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ gang yongs su dag pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams na/ sems can yongs su dag pa lta ci 'tshal gyi/ gang dag de ltar kun nas nyon mongs par gyur pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams de na se gol gtogs pa srid du yang
9b3(1): dad pa rnyed pa dang / se gol gtogs pa sring du yang sangs rgyas la su skyabasu 'gro ba dang / chos la skyabs su 'gro ba dang / dge 'dun la skyabs su 'gro ba dang / se gol gtogs pa srid du yang tshul khrims yang dag par bzung ste/ 
9b4(1): spyod pa 'di ni ches ngo mtshar to// de bas kyang gang dag se gol gtogs pa snying du yang 'dod chags dang bral ba la gnas pa'i sems yang dag par bzung ste gnas pa 'di rjes ngo mtshar to// de bas kyang gang dag se gol gtogs pa sring
9b5(1): du yang snying rje ba'i sems nye bar gzhag ste/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed pa 'di ni ches ngo mtshar to// byang chub sems dpa' de dag kyis gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das ngo mtshar to// bde bar gsheg pa ngo/ 
9b6(1): 'char to// de nas sgrib pa thams cad rnam spel ba la sogs pa byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyis bcom ldan 'das legs so// zhes gsol nas/ bco ldan 'ang de las 'di lta bu mthun pa'i rjes su bstan pa 'di mnyan nas/ 
9b7(1): bcom ldan 'das de'i zhabs la mgo bos phyag tshal te/ rang rang gi gnas nas dong ngo // dong nas bcom ldan 'das/ shAkya thub la tshong pa'i phyir/ la las ni rin po che'i shing meng tog dang bcas pa 'bram bu dang bcas pa/ chu dang zheng du ldan pa rnams
9b8(1): mngon par sprul la las ni bai Sha'i shing rnams/ la las ni shel gyi shing rnams/ la las ni dpag bsam gyi shing rnams/ laM las
10a1(1): nigaser kyogang rnams galas nim dgra gshong rnams/ la las ni 'azas bu nga rnams/ lasas dgas kyi hrI rnams/ lus sa mtshar gyi srid rnams/ sogs
10a2(1): spos kyi sprin rnams/ la las ni 'breng ba'i sprir rnams/ la las ni phye ma'i sprin rnams/ la las ni gdugs kyi sprin rnams/ la las ni rgyal mtshar gyi sprir rnams/ la las ni sil smar gyi
10a3(1): sprin rnams/ mngon par sprul to// mngon par sprul nas gcig tu 'dus te/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sgrib pa thams cad rnam par sel ba dang lhan cig tu mi 'jig rten gyi khams
10a4(1): ga la ba der dong ngo // de nas byang chub sems dpa' sgrib pa thams cad rnam par sel bas byang chub sems dpa' de dag la 'di skad ces smras so// kye ma'o grogs po dag mi mdzod kyi 'jig rten gyi kha

10b1(1): lus dang sems shin tu dga' bar byed pa khyung ste/ 'od des stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'di khyab cing snang bar gyur pa dang / gang stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi
10b2(1): khams 'di'i sems can dmyal ba pa'i lus su gnas pa dang / dud 'gro'i skye gnas pa'i lus su gnas pa dang / gshin rje'i 'jig rten pa'i lus su gnas pa de dag 'od des reg nas/ 
10b3(1): sdug bsngal gyi tshor ba dang bral te/ bde zhing khro ba dang gnod sems dang yang bral te/ phan tshun du pha mar 'du shes par gyur pa dang / gang yang stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams
10b4(1): 'di na 'jig rten gyi bar mun pa mun nag gang du nyi ma dang zla ba 'di ltar rdzu 'phrul che ba/ 'di ltar mthu che ba/ 'di ltar dbang che bar grags pa 'di dag gis kyang lham me/ lhan me
10b5(1): lhang nger ma gyur pa de dag kyang 'od des khyab nas/ snang bar gyur te/ gang der skyes pa'i sems can de dag kyang gcig gis gcig mthong ba dang / stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten
10b6(1): gyi khams 'di gang 'khor yug gi ri rnams dang / khor yug gi ri chen po rnams dang / ri btang bzung dang ri btang bzung chen po rnams dang / de ma yin pa'i ri nag po gzhan de dag kyang
10b7(1): 'od des khyab ste/ snang bar gyur pa dang / slar ni tshangs pa'i 'jig rten man cad 'og tu ni mnar med pa'i sems can dmyal ba chen po yan de'i bar du gang 'od des snang bar ma byas pa'i
11a1(1): sa phyogs de gang yang med pa de lta bu'i rdzu 'phrul mngon par bya ba mngon par byas so// de ma yin pa'i byang chub sems dpa' gzhan dag gis kyang ji lta bu'i rdzu 'phrul
11a2(1): mngon par bya ba mngon par byas pas/ zas 'dod pa'i sems can rnams ni zas tho ba/ btung ba 'dod pa rnams ni btung ba/ gos 'dod pa rnams ni gos/ bzhon pa 'dod pa rnams ni
11a3(1): banod pa/ nor 'dod pa napas ni ror zab/ yong ba rnam sa mig thob/ 'on pa rnams ni sgra thos/ sgren mo rnams nigs can du gyur/ myos pa rnams ni drang ba zag// sdug bcwa
11a4(1): bams ni bde bar gyur/ rnam ma rnams ni bang bar bcam pa de lta bu'i rdzu 'phrul mngor par bya ba mngar bar byas pa/ de nas slob pa thams cad rnam par mal ba la sogs pa byung
11a5(1): chub sems dpa' di dag thams cad yul ga ya dang / ga ya'i mgo'i rog la ba der nye ba dang / skyes bu dam pa de dag nye bar gyur ma thag tu stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig
11a6(1): rten gyi 'ams 'di rin po che'i dra bas khyabs par kun du sdang ngo // steng gi bar snang las kyang lha'i pad+ma'i tshar mngon par rab tu bab bo// lnga'i ma tog gi sprin rnams dang / lha'i
11a7(1): nga thog gi srir rnamapa dang / 'i bzang ba'i mi ma ma dang / rtswa'i sbos mo ni rnamapa dang / rtswa mas kyi smo rnam ma / stsam bya 'i sgor rnams kyi/  rnams sas
11b1(1): gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang / bdan gyi slar gyi char mngon par rab tu bab bo// de dag mngon par rab tu bab pas sems can gang la reg pa de dag thams cad rab tu bde bar 'gyur/ sum
11b2(1): ga ya dang ga ya mgo'o ri la shing tha mal pa dang / sa phyogs tha mal pa gang yod pa de dag kyang med par gyur par snang ngo // sa phyogs de dag na rin po che'i shing rnams dang / dpag bsam gyi
11b3(1): shing rnams dang / me tog gi shing rnams dang / 'bras bu'i shing rnams dang / can dar gyi shing rnams dang / a ga ru'i shing rnams kun tu snang ste/ de dag kun tu bzang por 'dug par gyur
11b4(1): to// bar snang na lha'i sil slar dag sgra 'byin cing / sil sran de dag las 'di lta bu'i tshigs su gcad pa 'di dag kyang byung ngo // lum po'i tshal re ba mchog tu gang skyes pa// mnyam med
11b5(1): gzhan yang nyon mongs dbang mi 'gyur// nam mkha' mtshungs mnyam de la phyag 'tshal 'dud// ri bo mchog rab 'di la bdag cag lhags/ byang chub mchog sus byang chub shing rab drung /

47b3(1): rtog pa 'di ni de'i bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// mchod pa dang / rim gro bya ba de dag nyid la gang sna tshogs pa 'di ni de'i shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ste/ rigs kyi bu de ltar na byang
47b4(1): chub sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs pa la mchod pa dang / rim gro bya ba'i thabs mkhas pa yin no// rigs kyi bu chos bcu po de dag dang ldan na// byang chub sems dpa' thabs mkhas pa

48a1(1): smon lam pa rnams yin/ yongs su mi skyo bo'i smon lam pa rnams yin/ legs par yongs su rdzogs pa'i smon lam pa rnams yin no// rigs kyi bu de de lta ji ltaran

48b1(1): khams ji sbed pa de dag thams cad byang chub tu sems bskyed du 'jug ste/ mthar gyis byang chub kyi spyad pa spyod du bcud nas/ byang chub kyi snying por 'dug pa rnams la mchod pa dang bkur ste rgyam
48b2(1): chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor bar gsol ba gdab po// yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba rnams kyang sems can la phan pa'i phyir bzhugs su gsol lo zhes smon lam 'debs te/ de ltar na byang
48b3(1): chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas thams cad kyis yang dag par bsngags pa'i smon lam pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' bdud thams cad shin tu tshar gcod pa'i smon lam pa yin zhe na/ 
48b4(1): 'di la byang chub sems dpa' 'di ltar bdag mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing na/ ci nas kyang bdud kyi sgra 'am/ bdud kyi ris kyi lha rnams 'byung bar yang mi 'gyur ba
48b5(1): de ltar bdag gis bya'o zhes smon lam 'debs te/ de ltar byang chub sems dpa' bdud thams cad shin tshar gcod pa'i smon lam pa yin/ ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' gzhan gyi dring mi 'jog
48b6(1): nga'i smon lam pa yin zhe na/ byang chub sems dpa' ni gzhan gyi dring la bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu smon lam mi 'debs kyi/ byang chub sems dpa' ni bdag nyid kyis shes rab kyis
48b7(1): dpyad de sems can gyi khams sdug bsngal ba la bltas nas// bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu smon lam 'debs te/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' gzhan gyi dring mi jog pa'i
49a1(1): smon lam pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' mtha' yas pa'i smon lam pa yin zhe na/ byang chub sems dpa' ni 'di lta ste/ byang chub kyi tshogs rnams kyi phyogs 'ag
49a2(1): zhig bzung nas/ nyi che ba'i smon lam mi 'debs kyi byang chub sems dpa' ni gla gos phrag pa gcig la gzar nas/ pus mo g.yas pa'i lhangs la btsugs te/ sems skyo bar byas nas/ phyogs
49a3(1): bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams rnams su bltas ste/ byang chub sems dpa' gang dag phyogs bcu na gnas pa dang / gang dag dka' ba spyod pa la gnas pa dang / gang dag byang chub kyi snying po la
49a4(1): gnas pa dang / sangs rgyas gang dag mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas pa dang / gang dag chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba de rnams la snying thag pa nas bsams te/ de dag gi chos bstan pa de snyed
49a5(1): pa de dag la mos par byed do// mos par gyur nas rjes su yi rang ngo // rjes su yi rang nas bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yongs su bsngo ste/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' 'tha'
49a6(1): pa'i smon lam pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems mi skrag pa'i smon lam pa yin zhe na/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' las dang po pa yin yang chos zab mo rnams thos pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi che ba zab mo
49a7(1): zos pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par rol pa zab mo thos pa dang / thabs la mkhas pa'i tshul zab mo thos kyang mi skrag mi dngas dngang bar mi 'gyur ro de 'di snyam du sangs rgyas kyi byang chub kyang la
49b1(1): yas sangs rgyas kyi yul yang mtha' yas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis sems can yongs su smon par mdzad pa yang mtha' yas te// de ni bdag 'dra bas shes par mi nus kyi/ sangs rgyas dag

49b3(1): zhe na/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' sems can dmu rgod sems can 'dul dka' bar rig pa ste/ de rnams kyis yi chad nas 'di lta bu'i dmu rgod 'di lta bu gdul dka' ba'i sems can 'di dag
49b4(1): gis chog go zhes ste/ de'i phyir yongs su skye zhing rgyab kyis phyogs par gyur te/ gang na sems can 'di lta bu dag gi mi thos pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams yongs su dag par smon lam 'debs so// sems can
49b5(1): gyi don la ma phyogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni yongs su dag pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams su skye bar yang mi 'gyur te/ de la byang chub sems dpa' shes rab can ni 'di ltar sems can gang rnams ngan pa
49b6(1): brtson 'grus chung ba/ blun pa blan pa khrag sngar zhugs pa'i rang bzhin can yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba'i chos can gyi khams ma lus pa 'di las btsugs pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad ring
49b7(1): sems dpa' thams cad kyis spangs par gyur pa yod pa de dag gi sangs rgyas kyi zhing du 'dus par gyur la/ bdag gis de dag byang chub kyi snying po la 'dug tu 'jug ste/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs
50a1(1): pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar bya'o snyam du sems bskyed de/ byang chub sems dpa' de ltar sems pa'i sems bskyed pa re re la yang bdud kyi gnas thams cad rab tu
50a2(1): g.yo'o// sangs rgyas thams cad kyang de'i bsngags pa gsung bar 'gyur ro// de sangs rgyas kyi zhing yang yongs su dag par 'gyur ro// bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyang myur tu mngon par
50a3(1): rdzogs par 'chang rgya ste// de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' yongs su mi skyo ba'i smon lam pa yin no// rigs kyi bu ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' legs par yongs su rdzogs pa'i smon lam pa yin ne/ 
50a4(1): rigs kyi bu 'di lta byang chub sems dpa' gang byang chub kyi snying po la 'dug ste/ bdud kyi dpung rnam par gzhom pa dang / bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba dang
50a5(1): yang de las par smon lam mi 'debs pa 'di ni legs par yongs su rdzogs pa'i smon lam pa zhes bya'o// 'di lta ste dper na mar ram 'bru mar gyi snod kha chang du gang ste/ lhag par rdul phra rab tsam gyi
50a6(1): thigags pa yang mi shong na/ de'i phyir e ma'o snod gang ba e ma'o snod shin gang ba zhes bya'o// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' byang chub mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas pa la/ smon lam legs

50b1(1): byang chub sems dpa' smon lam bu sumatshogs pa rnams yin no// rigs kyi bu chos bcu dang ldan na byang chub sems dpa' stobs phran sum tshogs pa rnams yin no// bcu grang zhen 'di lta sde ma
50b2(1): mi nor pa'i stobs phun sum tshogs pa rnams yin/ mi tshugs pa'i stobs phun sum tshogs pa rnams yin/ bsod nams kyi stobs phun sum tshogs pa rnams yin/ shes rab kyi stobs phun sum
50b3(1): tshogs pa rnams yin/ 'khor gyi stobs phur sum tshogs rnams yin/ rdzu 'phrul gyi stobs phun sum tshogs pa rnams yin/ dbang gi stobs phun sum tshogs pa rnams yin/ gzungs

51a1(1): dpa' bsod nams kyi stobs phun sum tshogs pa yin zhe na/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' ma bsgrubs pa'i bsod nams kyi tshogs 'jig rten pa'am/ 'jig rten las
51a2(1): 'das pa de gang med de/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' bsod nams kyi stobs phun sum tshogs pa rnams yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' shes rab kyi stobs phun sum tshogs pa yin
51a3(1): zhe na/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes ma gtogs par sangs rgyas kyi chos gang yang yar dag pa'i shes rab kyis ma mthong ba dang / mngon du ma byas pa dang / khong
51a4(1): dum chud pa de dag med de/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' shes rab kyi stobs phun sum tshogs pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' 'khor gyi stobs phur sum tshogs pa yin zhe na/ 
51a5(1): 'di la byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor tshul khrims nyams pa ma yin/ lta ba nyams pa ma yin/ cho ga nyams pa ma yin/ 'tshe ba nyams pa ma yin gyi/ byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor ni byang chub sem

51b1(1): gyi stobs bskyed pas mchog gis zil gyis gnon to// de 'dod na 'jam bu'i gling sgyu nyag ma gcig gis rtse mo la 'jog go/ de bzhin du gling bzhi pa dang / stong gi 'jig rten gyi khams dang /

51b6(1): bun sum tshogs pa yin zhe na/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' 'dod na/ stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams rin po che sna bdun gyis gang bar byin gyi brlob bo// de 'dong na brjod du/ 
51b7(1): med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi bar du rin po che rnam pa sna tshogs kyis/ yongs su gang bar byin gyis brlob ste/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' dbang gi stobs bun su/ 
52a1(1): tshogs pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' gzungs kyi stobs phun sum tshogs pa yin zhe na/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rang
52a2(1): rgyas kyi zhing dag na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das ji snyed cig don tha dad pa dang / tshig dang yi ge tha dad pa dang / brjod pa tha dad pa dang / tshul tha dad pa'i chos bshad pa de dag byang chub sems dpas/

52a4(1): na byang chub sems dpa' rnams par mi 'khrugs pa'i byin gyis brlabs kyi stobs phun sum tshogs pa yin zhe na/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams gtog/

52a6(1): byin gyis brlabs kyi stobs phun sum tshogs pa yin no// rigs kyi bu ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' bka' mi gcog pa'i stobs phun sum tshogs pa yin zhe na/ thabs mkhas pa ma gtogs pa/ 
52a7(1): gang byang chub sems dpa'i bka' ma gcig pa'i sems can re lta bu sems can gyings nam mthong ste/ rigs kyi bu de ltar na/ byang chub sems dpa' bka' mi gcog pa'i stobs phur sum chan
52b1(1): payin no// rigs kyi bu chos bcu po de dag dang ldanan byang chub sems dpa' stobs phun sum tshogs pa rnams yin no// rigs kyi bu chos bcu dang ldanan/ byang chub sems dpa' ye shes bran su mtshan
52b2(1): rnam yin no// bcu gang zhe na 'di lnga ste/ gang zag la bdag med pa'i ye shes phun sum tshogs pa rnams yin/ chos la bdag med pa'i ye shes phran sum tshogs pa rnams yin/ 'i che ba ma yin pa'i yi zhes/ 
52b3(1): phun sum tshogs pa rnams yin/ ting nge 'dzin gyi spyod yul gyi ye shes phun sum tshogs pa rnams yin/ byin gyi brlabs kyi ye shes phun sum tshogs pa rnams yin/ mi 'phrogs pa'i ye shes phun sum chog
52b4(1): pa rnams yin/ sems can thams cad kyi spyod pa la rnam par lta ba'i ye shes phun sum tshogs pa rnams yin/ lhun gyis grub pa'i ye shes phur sum pa rnams yin/ chos thams cad kyi mtshan nyid kyi
52b5(1): ye shes phun sum tshogs pa rnams yin/ 'jig rten las 'das pa'i ye shes phun sum tshogs pa rnams yin no// rigs kyi bu de la ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' gang zag la bdag med pa'i ye shes

52b7(1): rnams snying po med pa dang / byed pa med pa dang / gsog tu yang yang dag par mthong / phung po 'gag pa rnams 'jig par yang yang dag par mthong ste/ de 'di snyam du phung po 'di dag ni bdag med pa
53a1(1): sems can med pa/ srog med pa/ gso ba med pa/ gang zag med pa yin mod kyi 'on kyang byis pa so so'i skye bo bdag tu 'dzin pa la mngon par zhen pa 'di dag ni 'di ltar bdag
53a2(1): cag gi phung po rnams ni bdag go// bdag cag gi phung po rnams la bdag yod do// bdag cag gi bdag la phung po rnams yod do// bdag cag gi bdag ni phung po can no snyam ste/ de dag bdag tu
53a3(1): 'dzin pa la mngon par zhen pas de kho na nyid khong du mi chud do// de kho na nyid khong du ma chud pas mgal me'i 'khor lo ltar 'khor ba na 'khyam mo snyam du sems shing / de thams cad kyang byang chub sem
53a4(1): dpas yang dag pa de bzhin du rab tu shes te/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' gang zag la bdag med pa'i ye shes phun sum tshogs pa rnams yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' chos la
53a5(1): bdag med pa'i ye shes phun sum tshogs pa yin zhe na/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' chos su spro 'dogs pa dang / chos la bskur ba yang yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes te/ 'di snyam
53a6(1): du glo bur du byung ba'i chos la kun brtag pa'i ming gdags ste/ chos de yang de ngo bo nyid ma yin/ yi ge de dag kyang de ngo bo nyid ma yin mod kyi/ 'di ni ming tsam dang / tha snyad tsam du bya/ 
53a7(1): 'di la mngon par zhen par mi bya'o// glo bur du byung ba'i chos de yang thams cad kyi thams cad du med pa ma yin te/ gzhan gyi rkyen dang / gzhan gyi rkyen la bsdad pa dang / gzhan gyi rkyen
53b1(1): rnams 'byung zhing / rkyen dang bral na 'gag pa'i chos 'di ni yod do zhes de thams cad byang chub sems dpas yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes te/ de ltar na byang chub sems da
53b2(1): chos bdag med pa'i ye shes phun sum tshogs pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' nyi che ba ma yin pa'i ye shes phun sum tshogs pa yin zhe na/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa'
53b3(1): che ba'i ye shes skad cig gcig la 'jug cing / skad cig gnyis pa la 'jug pa ma yin gyi/ byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes mthong ba ni skad cig thams cad la thogs pa med par 'jug ste/ 
53b4(1): de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' nyi tshe ba ma yin pa'i ye shes phun sum tshogs pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' ting nge 'dzin gyi spyod yul gyi ye shes phun sum tshogs pa yin zhe
53b5(1): na/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' nyan thos kyi ting nge 'dzin rnams kyang rab tu shes/ rang sangs rgyas ting nge 'dzin rnams kyang rab tu shes/ byang chub sems dpa' ting nge 'dzin rnams kyang
53b6(1): rab tu shes/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i ting nge 'dzin rnams kyang rab tu shes// des ting nge 'dzin gang dang / ting nge 'dzin gyi spyod yul gang la nyan thos spyod pa de yang rab tu shes/ ting nge 'dzin
53b7(1): gang dang / ting nge 'dzin gyi spyod yul gang la rang sangs rgyas spyod pa rab tu shes/ ting nge 'dzin gang dang / ting nge 'dzin gyi spyod yul gang la byang chung sems dpa'i spong ba de yang rab tu shes
54a1(1): ting nge 'dzin gang dang / ting nge 'dzin gyi spyod yul gang la de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod pa de'ang rab tu shes te/ de bzhin gshegs pas skabs phye nas/ 
54a2(1): bzhin gshegs pa'i ting nge 'dzin rab tu shes kyi/ rnam par smin pas grub pa'i rang gi ye shes kyis ni ma yin no// ting nge 'dzin gzhan rnams ni par smin pas grub pa'i rang
54a3(1): ye shes kyis rab tu shes te/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' ting nge 'dzin gyi spyod yul gyi ye shes phur sum tshogs pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' byin gyis brlabs
54a4(1): kyi ye shes phun sum tshogs pa yin zhe na/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' nyan thos kyi byin gyi brlabs kyang ji lta bzhin du rab tu shes/ rang sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi brlabs kyang
54a5(1): blta ba bzhin du rab tu shes/ byang chub sems pa'i byin gyi brlabs kyang ji blta ba bzhin du rab tu shes na/ sems can de ma yin pa gzhan dag gi lta ci smos te/ de ltar na byang
54a6(1): chub sems dpa' byin gyi brlabs kyi ye shes phun sum tshogs pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' mi 'phrogs pa'i ye shes phun sum tshogs pa yin zhe na/ 'di la
54a7(1): byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes ni mu stegs can thams cad dang / bdud thams cad dang / nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyis mi 'phrogs pa yin te/ de ltar na byang chub
54b1(1): sems dpa' mi 'phrogs pa'i ye shes phun sum tshogs pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' sems can thams cad kyi spyod pa la rnam par lta ba'i ye shes phun sum tshogasapa
54b2(1): yin zhe na/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' ye shes yongs su dag pa dang / zhing rnyog pa med pas sems can gyi khams la rnam par lta ste/ des de na sems can la la byang chub tu sems
54b3(1): bskyed pa dag dang / lal byang chub sems ma bskyed pa dag dang / la la byang chub kyi sems bsgrubs pa dag dang / la la byang chub kyi sems ma bsgrubs pa dang / la las dang po la gnas
54b4(1): lalas bcu pa'i bar la gnas pa dag dang / la la mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas pa dag dang / la la mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas te chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor ba dag dang / 
54b5(1): la la bya ba kun byas te yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba dag dang / la la nyan thos kyi theg pas yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba dag dang / la la rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pas yongs su mya
54b6(1): ngan las 'da' ba dag dang / la la bde 'gror skye ba dag dang / la la ngan 'gror skye ba dag mthong ngo // de ltar sems can thams cad kyi spyod pa la rnam par lta ba ste/ de ltar na byang chub
54b7(1): sems dpa' sems can thams cad kyi skyed pa lo rnams par lta ba'i ye shes phun sum tshogs pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' lhun gyis grub pa'i ye shes phun sum tshogs
55a1(1): pa yin zhe na/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' spyod pa'am/ la sa 'am / 'gro ba 'am/ 'ong ba na lhun gyis grub cing ye shes 'byung te/ 'di lta ste dper na mi gnyid kyis
55a2(1): log pa'i dbugs 'byung ba dang rngub pa dag lhun gyis 'grub cing 'byung ngo // byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes de yang de bzhin du lta'o// ye shes de yang thams cad du mi chags par 'jug ste/ 
55a3(1): de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' lhun gyis grub pa'i ye shes phun sum tshogs pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' chos thams cad kyi mtshan nyid kyi ye shes phur sum tshogs pa yin zhen
55a4(1): 'di la byang chub sems dpas chos thams cad mtshan nyid mtshungs par yang rab tu shes/ mtshan nyid gcig par yang rab tu shes/ mtshan nyid du mar yang rab tu shes/ sgyu ma'i mtshan nyid du'ang
55a5(1): rab tu shes/ yang dag pa ma yin pa kun brtags pa'i mtshan nyid du'ang rab tu shes ste/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' chos thams cad kyi mtshan nyid kyi ye shes phun sum tshogs pa yin no// 
55a6(1): rigs kyi bu ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' 'jig rten las 'das pa'i ye shes phun sum tshogs pa yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di la byang chub sems dpa' zag pa med pa'i ye shes 'jig rten
55a7(1): thams cad las 'das pa dang ldan pa yin te/ rigs kyi bu de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' 'jig rten las 'das pa'i ye shes phun sum tshogs pa yin no// rigs kyi bu chos bcu po de dag dang
55b1(1): ldan na/ byang chub sems dpa' ye shes phun sum tshogs pa rnams yin no// rigs kyi bu chos bcu dang ldan na byang chub sems dpa' sa dang mtshungs pa rnams yin no// bcu gang zhe na 'di
55b2(1): ste/ yang shing chad med pa rnams yin/ sems can thams cad kyi 'tsho bar gyur pa rnams yin/ gnod pa dang lan du phar 'dogs pa dang bral ba rnams yin/ chos kyi sprin chen po kun zed pa rnams
55b3(1): yin/ sems can thams cad kyi gnas su gyur pa rnams yin/ dge ba'i chos rnams kyi sa bon gyi gzhir gyur pa rnams yin/ rin po che'i snod du gyur pa rnams yin/ rtsi chen po'i snod du gyur pa
55b4(1): rnams yin/ mi bskul ba rnams yin/ mi sdang ba rnams yin// rigs kyi bu de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' yangs shing tshad med pa yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ sa chen po tham
55b5(1): cad du yangs shing tshad med do// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang 'di lta ste/ bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs kyis kun du yangs shing tshad med pa yin te/ de ltar na byang chub sems
55b6(1): dpa' yangs shing chang med do// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' sems can thams cad kyi 'tsho bar gyur pa yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ sa chen pon 'di ltar yo byad rnam pa de dag na
55b7(1): sems can thams cad kyi 'tsho bar gyur pa yin no// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang sbyin pa dang / tshul khrims dang / bzod pa dang / brtson 'grus dang / bsam gtan dang / shes rab
56a1(1): la sogs pa byang chub kyi tshogs rnams dang / phan pa 'gyur ba'i yo byad rnam pa du ma de dang de dag gis sems can thams cad kyi 'tshe bar gyur pa yin te/ de ltar na byang chub sems
56a2(1): dpa' sems can thams cad kyi 'tshe bar yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' gnod pa dang / lan du phan 'dogs pa dang / bral ba yin zhe na/ 'di lta ste rigs kyi bu dper na sa chen po ni gnod pa
56a3(1): kyang zhe 'gras par 'gyur/ phan pas kyang rjes su chags par mi 'gyur te/ de la gnyis su 'du shes pa mi 'byung ngo // de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang gnod pa dag gis kyang zhe 'gras par
56a4(1): 'gyur/ phan pa dgra gis kyang rjes su chags par mi 'gyur te/ de ni sems can de dag la rjes su chags pa dang / khong khro ba yang mi skye ste/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' gnod pa dang lan du phan 'dog
56a5(1): pa dang bral ba yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi sprin chen po kun rked pa yin ne na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na sa chen po ni sprin chen po las bab pa'i chu'i klung chen po kun zer de/ 
56a6(1): bzod cing kun 'dzin to// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang de bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi sprin chen po las chos kyi 'ong ba chen po rab tu phab pa kun zed cing bzod pa 'dzin te/ de ltar na byang chub sem
56a7(1): dpa' chos kyi sprin can pan zad pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' sems can thams cad kyi gnas su gyur pa yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ sa chen po ni sems can thams cad dang / 
56b1(1): 'gro ba dang / 'ong ba'i gnas su gyur pa yin no// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang sems can thams thams cad kyi bde 'gro dang / mya ngan las 'das par 'gro ba'i gnas su 'gyur ba yin/ de ma
56b2(1): byang chub sems dpa' sems can thams cad kyi gnas su gyur pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' dge ba'i chos kyi sa bon gyi gzhir gyur pa yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ mtho
56b3(1): thams cad ni sa chen po gzhir gyur pa las skye'o// de bzhin du sems can thams cad kyi dge ba'i chos kyi sa bon thams cad kyang byang chub sems dpa' gzhir gyur pa las skye ste/ de ltar na byang chub
56b4(1): sems dpa' dge ba'i chos kyi sa bon gyi gzhir gyur pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' rin po che'i snod du gyur pa yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na sa chen po ni rin po che rnam pasdu
56b5(1): tshogs kyi snod yin te/ sa chen po la rin po che sna tshogs kun snang ngo // de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang yon tan rin po che rnam pa sna tshogs kyi snod du gyur pa yin te/ byang chub sems
56b6(1): dpa' la yon tan rin po che sna tshogs kun snang ste/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' rin po che'i snod du gyur pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' rtsi chen po'i snod du gyur pa yin zhem
56b7(1): rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper ni/ rtsi chen po gang dag nang rnam pa sna tshogs zhi bar gyur pa dag kyang sa chen po la gnas te 'jig rten na snang ngo // de bzhin du gang dag gis nyon mongs pa'i nang rnam
57a1(1): pa sna chags pa rnams ni par 'gyur ba tshas kyi chen pa rnams kyang byang chub ses dpa su sa dang 'jig rten du 'byung ba gyuraH/ den rang byang chub sems dpa
57a2(1): ci chen po'i snod du gyur pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' mi bskal ba yin nen/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na sa chen po ni 'di ltar sha sdang dang sbrang bu dang / rlung dang /  mdang
57a3(1): sbrul gyis reg pa'i sdug bsngal thams cad kyis mi bskul ba yin no// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang 'di lta ste/ sems can thams cad las byung ba'i phyir nang gi sdug bsngal thams
57a4(1): cad kyis mi bsgral ba yin te/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' mi bskul ba yin no// rigs kyi bu ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' mi sdang ba yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na sa chen
57a5(1): po ni glang po'i rgyal po dang / ri dgas kyi rgyal po rnam pa sna tshogs kyi sgra thos kyang mi skrag mi dngang dngang bar mi 'gyur ro// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' bdud dang mu stegs thams cad kyi
57a6(1): sgra thos na mi skrag mi dngang dngang bar mi 'gyur te/ rigs kyi bu de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' mi sdang ba yin no// rigs kyi bu chos bcu po de dag dang ldan na/ byang chub sems dpa' sa
57a7(1): chen po dang mtshungs pa rnams yin no// rigs kyi bu bcu dang ldan na byang chub sems dpa' chu dang mtshungs pa rnams yin no// bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ dge ba'i chos la gzhol ba rnams
57b1(1): yin/ dkar po'i chos thams cad bskyed pa rnams yin/ dga' ba dang / dad pa dang / rangs pa'i gsher ba can rnams yin/ nyon mongs pa'i rtsa ba'i rgyun thams cad srung ba rnams yin/ dngas/ 
57b2(1): zhing rnyog pa med de gsal ba rnams pa rnams yin/ nyon mongs pa'i yongs su gdung ba rab tu zhi bar byed pa rnams yin/ 'dod pa la srid pa zlogs rnams pa yin/ zab cing gting dpag
57b3(1): ba rnams yin/ mthong maran 'gengs pa rnams yin/ nyon mongs pa'i rdul thams cad rab tu zhi bar byed pa rnams yin no// rigs bu 'di ltar na byang chub sems dge ba'i chos la gnol ba yin
57b4(1): zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ chu ni gzhol bar 'gro ba dang / gzhol bar rgyu ba yin no// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang dge ba'i chos la gzhol zhing dge ba'i chos kyi phyir
57b5(1): rgyu ba yin te/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' dge ba'i chos la gzhol ba yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' dkar po'i thams cad bskyed pa yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dpe
57b6(1): na chu ni rtswa dang / shing gel ba dang / rtsi dang nags tshal thams cad bskyed de/ skyes pa rnams kyang phyir zhing rgyas par byed do// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang ting nge 'dzin gyi chus byang / 
57b7(1): kyi phyogs kyi chos thams cad rnam par bskyed do// skyes pa rnams kyang thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi shing du gyur gyi bar du phyir zhing rgyas par byed do// thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi shing du gyur pa
58a1(1): ngag gis sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi 'bras bu rnam pa sna tshogs dag gis sems can rnams 'tsho bar 'gyur te/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' dkar po'i chos thams cad
58a2(1): bskyed pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' dga' ba dang / dad pa dang / rangs pa'i gsher ba can yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na chun ngo bo nyid kyis gsher ba can te/ gzhan
58a3(1): yang gsher bar byed do// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang ngo bo nyid kyis dga' ba dang / rangs pa'i gsher ba can yin te/ sems can gzhan yang dga' ba dang / dad pa dang / rangs pa'i
58a4(1): gsher ba can du byed do// de la dga' ba ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos tshol ba'o// dad pa ni sangs rgyas dang / chos dang / dge 'dun la rten pa'o// rangs pa ni gang sems dag pa ste/ de ltar
58a5(1): na byang chub sems dpa' dga' ba dang / dad pa dang / rangs pa'i gsher ba can yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' nyon mongs pa'i rtsa ba'i rgyun thams cad srung ba yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di
58a6(1): 'di lta ste dper na/ chu ni shing gi rnam pa dang / rtsa'i rnam pa'i rtsa ba dag gi/ rgyun rnams srung lo// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang bsgom pa la gnas pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi chus nyon mongs
58a7(1): nga'i rtsa ba'i rgyun thams cad sprul te/ ji ltar nyon mongs pa'i rtsa ba'i rgyun 'di dag gi ming yang shes pa dang / nyon mongs pa'i dring ba'i bag chags kyang med par 'gyur ba de lta bur sprul te/ de ltar
58b1(1): na byang chub sems dpa' nyon mongs pa'i rtsa ba'i rgyun thams cad sprul pa yin no// ji ltar nad ngang zhing / rnyog pa med de gsal ba yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na chu ni rang bzhin gyis dang ning
58b2(1): rnyogs pa med de gsal lo// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang rang bzhin gyis dang zhing rnyog pa med de gsal ba yin no// de la bag la nyal ba dang kun ras ldang ba dang bral bas na dang ba'o// 'dod
58b3(1): chags dang zhe sdang dang / gti mug dang bral bas na rnyog pa med pa'o// dbang po rab tu dang bas ma gsal ba ste/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' dang zhing rnyog pa med de gsal ba yin no// ji lta na byang
58b4(1): chub sems dpa' nyon mongs pa'i yongs su gdung ba rab tu zhi bar byed ce na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na chu ni sa chen po dpyid kyi tsha bas gdungs pa dang / de las gzhan yang sems can rnam
58b5(1): dpyid kyi tsha bar gdungs pa rnams rab tu zhi bar byed do// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang nyon mongs pas gdungs pa'i sems can gyi khams thams cad chos kyi chus rab tu zhi bar byed de/ 
58b6(1): de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' nyon mongs pas yongs su gdungs po rab tu zhi bar byed pa'o// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' 'dod pa la srid pa bzlog pa yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper
58b7(1): na chu yi sgom pas nyen pa'i sems can rnams kyi sdom pa rnam par bzlog go// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang yul la srid pas nyen pa'i sems can nyen par gyur pa dag la gang gis sem
59a1(1): can de dag gi yul la sred pa ldog par 'gyur ba de lta bu'i chos kyi char mngon par 'bebs te/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' 'dod pa la sred pa bzlog par byed de/ 
59a2(1): ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' zab cing gting dpag dka' ba yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ chu'i 'dzings ni zab cing gting dpag dka' ba yin no// de bzhin du byang chub sem
59a3(1): dpa' ye shes yang dag par grub pa yang 'di lta ste/ bdud thams cad dang / mu stegs can thams cad kyis gting dpag dka' zhing zab pa yin te/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' zab cing ga
59a4(1): dpag bka' ba yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' mtho dman 'gengs pa rnams yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ chu yi klung ni sa'i phyogs mthon dman 'grengs so// de
59a5(1): bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang chos kyi chu yi klung gis sems can gyi khams mthon dman 'gengs te// ji ltar chus 'gengs pa ltar sems can la gnod par byed pa de lta bu byang chub
59a6(1): sems dpa' ma yin gyi/ sems can de rnams la snying brtse ba'i phyir chos kyi chu yi klung 'bebs shing / de dag la gnod par mi byed do// de ltar byang chub sems dpa' mthon dman 'gengs
59a7(1): pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' nyon mongs pa'i rdul thams cad rab tu zhi bar byed pa yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ chus ni sa'i phyogs snyam zhing rdul 'thul ba
59b1(1): thams cad snum par byed cing rdul de dag zhi bar byed do// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang sems can sems brngub pa rnams 'di lta ste shes rab la gnas pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi chus sem
59b2(1): snum par byed cing sems can de dag gi nyon mongs pa'i rdul thams cad rab tu zhi bar byed do// de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' nyon mongs pa'i rdul thams cad rab tu zhi bar byed pa yin no// 
59b3(1): rigs kyi bu chos bcu po de dag dang ldan na byang chub sems dpa' chu dang chungs pa rnams yin no// rigs kyi bu chos bcu dang ldan na/ byang chub sems dpa' me dang mtshungs pa rnams yin no/ 
59b4(1): bcu gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ nyon mongs pa'i phyag dar khrod pa thams cad sreg par byed/ sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams kyang yongs su smin par byed/ nyon mongs pa'i 'dam thams cad kyang skam
59b5(1): par byed/ me'i phung po dang 'dra ba rnams yin/ spang bar gyur pa rnams yin/ skrag par byed pa rnams yin/ dbugs 'byin pa rnams yin/ sems can thams cad kyi thun mong du gyur pa rnams
59b6(1): yin/ mchod par byed pa rnams yin/ mi brnyas par byed pa rnams yin/ rigs kyi bu de la ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' nyon mongs pa'i phyag dar khung thams cad sreg ce na rigs kyi bu 'di
59b7(1): lha ste dper na me ni phyag dar khrong dang rtswa dang / shing dang / gel ba dang / rtsi dang / sdong po thams cad sreg go// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang shes rab kyis bag la nyal ba dang / kun na
60a1(1): ldang ba dang / 'dod chags dang / zhe sdang dang / gti mug gi nyon mongs pa'i phyag dar khung thams cad sreg ste/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' nyon mongs pa'i phyag dar rung
60a2(1): thams cad sreg pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad yongs su smin par byed ce na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na me ni lo tog dang / rtsi dang sdong po'i rnam pa/ 
60a3(1): thams cad yongs su smin par byed/ de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang shes rab kyis nang gi sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams yongs su smin par byed pa'ang ji ltar 'jig par mi 'gyur ba de ltar yongs su
60a4(1): smin par byed do// de ltar na sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams yongs su smin par byed pa'o// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' nyon mongs pa'i 'dam thams cad skam par byed ce na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ 
60a5(1): me ni ru brar gyi 'dam thams cad skam par byed do// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang shes rab kyis zag pa nyon mongs pa'i 'jam thams cad sam par byed de/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' 'on
60a6(1): mongs pa'i 'dam thams cad skam par byed do// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' me'i phung po dang 'dra ba yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ sems can grang ba'i nad kyi nyen pa rnams kyi grang ba med
60a7(1): par bya ba'i phyir me'i phung po byed do// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang nyon mongs pa'i grang ba'i nad kyis btab pa'i sems can rnams kyi nyon mongs pa'i grang nang med par bya ba'i phyir shes rab kyis
60b1(1): rab tu dro bar byed de/ de ltar nga byang chub sems dpa' me'i phung po dang 'dra ba yin no// de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' snang bar gyur pa yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper nags kyi rtse mong
60b2(1): ri 'bigs byed kyi rtse mo na me'i phung po chen po 'bar ba des dpag chad gcig kho ra khor yug tu snang bar byed/ dpag tshad gnyis khor khor yug dang / dpag tshad gsum khor khor yug tu yang spang byed do// 
60b3(1): de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang ye shes kyi snang bas dpag chad brgyar yang khyab par byed/ dpag chad stong du'ang khyab par byed/ dpag chad stong phrag brgyar yang khyab par byed pa nas/ 'jig
60b4(1): rten gyi khams dpag tu med grangs med pa'i bar du yang khyab par byas nas/ sems can thams cad la ye shes kyi snang bar byed de/ ye shes kyi snang ba des mi shes pa'i mum pa mun nag thams cad rnam par
60b5(1): sel te/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' snang bar gyur pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' skrag par byed pa yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na ri dgas khro bo 'am/ ri dgas kyi rgyal
60b6(1): po khro bos me'i phung po chen po mthong na skrag cing dngangal dngang bar gyur cing / 'di lta ste me'i 'jigs pas sdug pas gnas de ring bas kyang shin tu ring bar spong ngo // de bzhin du bdud rnams sam/ bdud
60b7(1): kyi ris kyi lha rnams kyis byang chub sems dpa' mthong na skrag cing dngang la dngang par gyur cing / 'di lta ste gzi brjid chung ba'i phyir gang du byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ma zlos na mthong ba kyi
61a1(1): smos kyang ci dgos par ring bas shin du ring bar sa'i phyogs de yongs su spong ngo // de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' skrag par byed pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa'
61a2(1): dbugs 'byin pa yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na mi la la zhig 'brog dgon par 'khyams pa las me'i phung po chen po mthong ste/ de de'i logs su song ba dang / des de grong ngam rje'u brang
61a3(1): mthong nas de shugs phyin de rab tu dbugs phyin nas/ 'jig pa thams cad dang bral bar 'gyur ro// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang 'khor ba'i 'brog dgon par 'khyams pa'i sems
61a4(1): can rnams kyis byang chub sems dpa' mthong na/ shugs phyin par 'gyur rab tu dbugs phyin par 'gyur/ nyon mongs pa'i 'jigs pa thams cad dang bral bar 'gyur te/ de ltar na byang chub se/ 
61a5(1): dpa' dbugs 'byin pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' sems can thams cad kyi thun mong du gyur pa yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste na me ni sems can thams cad kyi mthun mong du
61a6(1): gyur pa ste/ ji ltar na rgyal po la phan par nye bar gnas pa ltar gdol bu la yang de bzhin no// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang sems can thams cad kyi thun mong du gyur yin te/ ji ltar rgyal
61a7(1): pil phan pa nye bar gnas pa ltar gdal bral yang de bzhin te/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' sems can thams cad dang thun med du gyur pa yin no// ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' mchar par/ 
61b1(1): bya ba yin nan/ rims kyi bu 'di sa snyed per na melan tham pa dang / rgyal rigs dang / zang rdal ci mi dang / rdul gyi mi rnams kyis mchod // de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' na
61b2(1): lnga dang / mi dang / lA ma yin dang / dri zar bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyis ston par 'du shes pas mchod do// de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' mchod par bya ba yin no// ji ltar nami bcas
61b3(1): yin ne na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ me sdug chung ngu yang tshig pa'i bdag nyid yin no// de bzhin du mos par spyod pa la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' mthu slo bas ma rnyed brjen
61b4(1): ba chen po la las dang po pa yang lha dang / mi dang lA ma yin bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyis mi brnyas pa yin no// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / lha ma yin
61b5(1): rnams kyis byang chub sems dpa' 'di ring por mi thogs par byang chub kyi snying po la 'dug ste/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar khong du chud
61b6(1): de/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' mi brnyas pa yin no// rigs kyi bu chos bcu po de dag dang ldan na byang chub sems dpa' me dang mtshungs pa rnams yin no// rigs kyi bu chos bcu dang ldan
61b7(1): na byang chub sems dpa' rlung dmar dang mtshungs pa rnams yin no// bcu gang zhe na 'di lta ste gnas med par spyod pa dang / spyod yul kun tu mu med pa dang / sems cad nga rgyal gyis snyems

63a5(1): ba'i bsal pa thams cad du'ang rgyul/ chos kyi lus kyis mi snang ba yang ma yin zhing / mi rtog rnam par mi rtog ste/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' gnas med par spyod pa yin no// rigs
63a6(1): kyi bu ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' spyod yul kun tu mu med pa yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na rlung dmar ni phyogs bcu'i 'jig kyi khams dpag tu med pa dag tu reg par byed/ 
63a7(1): de g.yo ba cing rgya'o// rigs kyi bu de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' rlung dmar yang chos mu med pa dag kun rdzob dang / don dam par kun nas mthong zhing rgyas par byed/ rig par bye

63b2(1): pa dang ldan zhing phyogs thams cad kyi mthar thug pa'i spyod bral bar gyur nas/ rgyu zhing 'gro ste/ rigs kyi bu de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' spyod yul kun tu mu med pa yin no// rigs kyi bu
63b3(1): ji ltar ni byang chub sems dpa' sems can nga rgyal gyis sems pa'i rtse mo 'thor zhing 'jig la rab tu sel bar byed pa ma yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta steng por na rlung ngamar ni ri dang / 
63b4(1): dang nags tshal gyi rtse mo dag 'dug par byed/ rab tu snyil bar byed/ rnam par 'jig par byed/ 'thor bar byed/ mi snang bar byed do// de bzhin du byang sems dpa' rlung dmar yang
63b5(1): sems can nga rgyal dang / rlom pa dang / dregs pa dang / 'jig tshogs la lta ba'i rtse mos snyems pa rnams gzugs dang / daral bab pa dang / longs spyod dang / dbang dang / stobs
63b6(1): dang / che dang / nad med pa dang / 'tsho ba dang / bzod pa dang / thos pa dang / yid gzhungs pa dang / g.yog dang / smra mkhas pa dang / dpal che ba'i dregs par myos pa dag dang / yang
63b7(1): dag pa'i nan tan gyis bdag spong ba rnams la de dang khyad zhugs pa'i phun sum tshogs pa bstan pa dang / chos bstan pas nga rgyal choms par byed cing / dge ba dri ma med pa la sbyor bar
64a1(1): byed de/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' sems can dkyil gyis snyems pa'i rtse mo 'thor zhing 'jig la rab tu spel bar byed pa yin no// rigs kyi bu ji ltar na
64a2(1): byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi char sprin chen po kun nas bskyed pa yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na/ rlung dmar ni phyogs bzhi nas/ sprin gyi dkyil 'khor kha dog sna tshogs
64a3(1): can dang / zab cing gsal la mnyen zhing 'jam pa'i 'brug sgra rgya mtsho'i dbyangs can klu ro sna tshogs kyi sgra 'byid cing yid du 'ong ba'i dbyangs rjes su grags pa/ srog gi 'phreng ba'i rgyan
64a4(1): gyis rnam par brgyan pa/ gang dag gis 'jig rten gyi khams bye ba khrag khrig stong phrag brgyad dag kun nas yongs su khyebs par byas te/ 'gro ba thams cad dga' ba dang / le tog dang sngo
64a5(1): bo yongs su bskyed pa'i char gyi rgyun rin po che rtag tu rgyun ma'i chang par mngon par 'byebs pa'i sprin chen po kun nas spang ngo // de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang rlung dmar ya
64a6(1): lus sna tshogs kyi sprin sems can thams cad dga' bar byed pa/ phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams mtha' yas ma med pa snang bar byed pa/ 'od zer kha dog mtha' yas pa'i
64a7(1): klog gi 'phreng ba'i rgyun 'byung ba yang dag pa de khon nyid kyi chos kyi 'brug sa yan lag stong phrag drug nubar sgrog pa/ snying rje chen po'i rlung dmar gyis yang dag par mtho ba/ chos kyi
64b1(1): kyi dbyings kyis mtha' klas pa'i 'gro ba thams cad kyi nam mkha' khyab par byed dag gis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kun nas khebs par byas shing ngan song dang / mi khom
64b2(1): ba la sogs nas sems can rnams rnam par bslang ste/ rnam pa thams cad du mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po dang / 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gyi snang ba rnam par dag pa yang byin gyis brlab/ 
64b3(1): te/ bkod pa thams cad kyi rgyan gyis brgyan pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams dag kyang byin gyis brlabs nas/ lha dang / mi dga' ba dang / mgri ba dang / rangs pa mchog tu gyur pas dang
64b4(1): ba dang / bde ba mchog thob pa dang ldan pa rnams kyi 'jig rten pa dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos dkar po'i lo tog dang / rtsi chen po dang sdong po thams cad rnam par bskyed pa dang / 
64b5(1): thams cad du bskyed par chos kyi dbang bskur ba'i phyir sems can thams cad kyi phun sum tshogs pa dang dga' bar byed pa dang / rgud pa rab tu zhi bar byed pa'i chos kyi char chen po
64b6(1): mngon par 'bebs te/ rigs kyi bu de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' chos kyi char sprin chen po kun nas bskyed pa yin no// rigs kyi bu ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' 'gro ba
64b7(1): thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa'i gdung ba rab tu zhi bar byed pa yin zhe na/ rigs kyi bu 'di lta ste dper na rlung ngomar dri zhim po'i char gyi rgyun gyi snying po cam ldang na/ sems can gyi gas

65b5(1): pa rnam par phye ba sna tshogs mngon par bsgrub bo// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' rlung dmar yang phyogs bcu kun tu sems can thams cad kyi bsod nams kyi phung po phur sum chog

65b7(1): gling chen po bzhi pa dang / ro rab phun sum tshogs pa de ltar ni nyan thos kyi phun sum tshogs pa rnams blta'o// ji ltar stong gi 'jig rten gyi khams phun sum tshogs pa de ltar ni spangs
67a1(1): re re'i 'jig rten gyi khams gang+gA'i klung grangs med pa'i bye ma snyed du rtogs pa'i brgya byin rnams kyi bsod nams kyi phung po ci tsam pa de dang / brgya byin gcig ldan par gyur

67a3(1): 'dra ba sha stag tu gyur la/ bgrang ba de nyid kyis phyogs bcu'i phyogs re re'i 'jig rten gyi khams gang gang+gA'i grangs med pa'i bye ma snyed du gtags pa'i sems can de dag thams cad tshangs

67a7(1): kyi brang btsatsam pa de dus gsum gyi na ma mkhas pas su gtogs pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams su gtogs pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rdul pa rab brgyar bskur bas/
